 The main points of the draft Lokpal Bill, which are going to take shape after waiting for more than four decades, are as follows: 1
 pradhanmantri or nyaaypalika lokapal ke daayre main nahin rahenge
 2
 pradhanmantri padmukt hone ke baad lokapal ke daayre main aayenge
 3
 pad par rahete hue pradhanmantri ke khilaaf bhrashtachar kii koi bhi shikaayat saat saal tak maanya rahegi
 If he is relieved within seven years of receiving the complaint, then the investigation against him will be started
 4
 The conduct of mps within Parliament is also excluded from the purview of Lokpal
 5
 The Lokpal will have a chairman and eight other members
 iske aadhe sadsy nyaaypalika se honge
 6
 lokapal ko padmukt hone ke baad kabhi bhi kisi bhi dal se chunaav ladane kaa adhikaar nahin hoga
 7
 ucchtam nyaayalay ke kisi sevarat yaa sevanivrutt nyaayadhish yaa ucch nyaayalay ke koi sevarat yaa sevanivrutt mukhya nyaayadhish ko lokapal kaa adhyaksh banaaya ja saktaa he
 8
 lokapal ke sadsy ke rup main niyukt hone vaale gaiyr-nyaayik prishthbhumi vaale logon ke liye puri tarah eemaandaar hona or prashasan main bhrashtachar nirodhi nigaraanee ke kaam kaa kam se kam 25 varsh kaa anubhav hona jaruri hoga
 9
 lokapal ko swat: sangyaan ke aadhaar par nirnay karne ke adhikaar honge
 10
 lokapal kii nishpakshta banaaye rakhane ke liye iske sadasyon main kisi bhi raajnneetik dal ke logon ko shaamil nahin kiya jaayegaa
 11
 lokapal kaa chayan pradhanmantri kii adhyakshata vaali samiti karegi
 The committee will consist of the Speaker of the Lok Sabha, the Chairman of the Rajya Sabha, the Leader of the Opposition in the Lok Sabha and the Rajya Sabha, a member of the Cabinet and one Judge each of the Supreme Court and the High Court
 12
 The President will have the right to remove the Lokpal
 raashtrapati kii ore se pradhan nyaayadhish ko sifarish ke liye maamla bheja jaayegaa
 The final decision will be of the President
 13
 The Ombudsman will have the right to select his staff-officers
 14
 The CBI will not be placed under the Lokpal but will be able to take the services of CBI officials
 15
 The Ombudsman will not have to seek approval under the Criminal Penal Code Code and the anti-corruption Act to investigate cases that may be prosecuted in future
 16
 The Lokpal will also have the right to confiscate the property of corrupt bureaucrats

 bijepi madh nishedya or utpaada vibhaag ke is bill kaa virodh karegi
 When this new bill is passed, the laws on liquor prohibition in Bihar will become more stringent
 is sthiti main bihar main sharaab pinaa, bechnaa, rakhana or banane par kadaa pratibandh lagegaa
 Although the law of prohibition in Bihar was already very strict since April, but it is being made more stringent
 kanoon ko or sakht banane kii taiyaarisharabbandi ko lekar prastaavit nae kanoon main yah praavdhaan he ki agarsharabko lekar kisi gaanv main police ne chhapemari kii or uskaa gaanvvaalon ne virodh kiya to us sthiti main puure gaanv par samuhik rup se mukadmaa chalaaya jayega
 If alcohol is being produced in a village, then action will be taken under the law, assuming the entire village is responsible for it
 bihar main duusare rajyon se sharaab kii taskari jaridarasal bihar main april maah se sharaab par purna pratibandh lagaaya gaya he
 Despite this, the flow of liquor from neighboring states and Nepal to Bihar continues to grow

 sarkaar inako chinhit kar karrwai karen
